In reply to this message
Bogdan, you asked about tag "run", Gatling, Grafana, and InfluxDB.

I used InfluxDB 1.8 (old version)
with example config:
https://github.com/polarnik/gatling-grafana-dashboard/blob/master/devenv/influxdb.conf#L429-L436
  "v2.gatling.*.*.*.users.*.*      .measurement.run.host.simulation.measurement.request.field",
  "v2.gatling.*.*.*.*.*.*   .measurement.run.host.simulation.request.status.field   group=0",
In this case:
- "v2" prefix is skipping
- "gatling" is measurement
- first "*" is "run" tag
- second "*" is "host" tag

If you are using InfluxDB 2.0 then you could configurate:
telegraf: https://www.influxdata.com/time-series-platform/telegraf/
with config section "inputs.socket_listener":
- https://docs.influxdata.com/telegraf/v1.21/plugins/#socket_listener
- https://github.com/influxdata/telegraf/blob/release-1.21/plugins/inputs/socket_listener/README.md
with data format "graphite":
- https://github.com/influxdata/telegraf/tree/master/plugins/parsers/graphite
[[inputs.socket_listener]]
  service_address = "tcp://:2003"
  data_format = "graphite"
  separator = "."
  templates = [
  "gatling.*.users.*.*      measurement.simulation.measurement.request.field",
  "gatling.*.*.*.*   measurement.simulation.request.status.field   group=0",
  "v2.gatling.*.*.*.users.*.*      .measurement.run.host.simulation.measurement.request.field",
  "v2.gatling.*.*.*.*.*.*   .measurement.run.host.simulation.request.status.field   group=0"
  ]
And with config section outputs.influxdb_v2
- https://docs.influxdata.com/telegraf/v1.21/plugins/#influxdb_v2
- https://github.com/influxdata/telegraf/blob/release-1.21/plugins/outputs/influxdb_v2/README.md
!! But the dashboard did not check with InfluxDB 2.0. InfluxDB 2.* could be using like InfluxDB 1.* but I did not check it.

Also I used Gatling with config (gatling.conf):
      rootPathPrefix = "gatling" # The common prefix of all metrics sent to Graphite
      rootPathPrefix = ${?GATLING_PREFIX}
      rootPathPrefix = ${?gatling.rootPathPrefix}
In this case:
- "gatling" is default value of rootPathPrefix
- If environment variable or property "GATLING_PREFIX" is not empty then value of "GATLING_PREFIX" is value of rootPathPrefix
- If environment variable or property "gatling.rootPathPrefix" is not empty then value of variable is value of rootPathPrefix

Also, I used sh/bat-file with environment variable set or custom Engine script for debugging.
See end of description on page https://grafana.com/grafana/dashboards/9935

templates = [
"gatling.*.users.*.* measurement.simulation.measurement.request.field run=0,host=local",
"gatling.*.*.*.* measurement.simulation.request.status.field group=0,run=0,host=local",
"v2.gatling.*.*.*.users.*.* .measurement.run.host.simulation.measurement.request.field",
"v2.gatling.*.*.*.*.*.* .measurement.run.host.simulation.request.status.field group=0"
]


In this config default values have been used
run=0
host=local
group=0

1. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç–µ InfluxDB 2.0 —Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ...
from(bucket: v.bucket)
|> range(start: v.timeRangeStart, stop: v.timeRangeStop)
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_measurement"] == "events")
|> filter(fn: (r) => r["_field"] == "text")

*************************************************************************************************

2. –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏–∑ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ "log.jtl"
$JmeterLogContent = (Get-Content -Path "log.jtl" -Head 2) + (Get-Content -Path "log.jtl" -Tail 1) | ConvertFrom-Csv
$TimeFirst = [System.DateTimeOffset]::FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(($JmeterLogContent[0].timeStamp))
$TimeLast = [System.DateTimeOffset]::FromUnixTimeMilliseconds(($JmeterLogContent[1].timeStamp))
$TotalSeconds = [math]::Round(($TimeLast - $TimeFirst).TotalSeconds, 0)

$DataFormat = 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'
$Output = $($($TimeFirst.LocalDateTime.ToString('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')) + "`n" + $($TimeLast.LocalDateTime.ToString('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')))

Write-Host "TotalSeconds: $TotalSeconds"
Write-Host $Output

$Output | Out-File 'time.txt' -Verbose

Write-Host 'Copy text to the clipboard' -ForegroundColor Yellow
Set-Clipboard -Value $Output

*************************************************************************************************

3. –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏–∑ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ "jmeter.log"

$FilePath = Join-Path -Path $PSScriptRoot -ChildPath '.\bin\jmeter.log'

$JmeterLogContent = ( Select-String -Path $FilePath -Pattern 'JMeterMenuBar: setRunning|Running the test!|Notifying test listeners of end of test' ).Line

# GUI
# Start
# 2019-10-14 19:42:55,612 INFO o.a.j.g.u.JMeterMenuBar: setRunning(true, *local*)
# Stop
# 2019-10-14 19:43:12,310 INFO o.a.j.g.u.JMeterMenuBar: setRunning(false, *local*)

# CONSOLE
# Start
# 2022-03-16 09:09:33,484 INFO o.a.j.e.StandardJMeterEngine: Running the test!
# Stop
# 2022-03-16 10:44:27,208 INFO o.a.j.e.StandardJMeterEngine: Notifying test listeners of end of test


$FormatString = 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss,fff'
$TimeFirst = $null
$TimeLast = $null
foreach ( $Line in $JmeterLogContent ) {
if ( -not $TimeFirst ) {
$TimeFirst = [datetime]::ParseExact( $Line.Substring( 0, 23 ), $FormatString, [System.Globalization.CultureInfo]'ru-ru')
}
else {
$TimeLast = [datetime]::ParseExact( $Line.Substring( 0, 23 ), $FormatString, [System.Globalization.CultureInfo]'ru-ru')
$TotalSeconds = [math]::Round(( $TimeLast - $TimeFirst ).TotalSeconds, 0 )
Write-Host "[<-] Start: $( $TimeFirst.ToString( 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss' ))"
Write-Host "[tt] Total: $TotalSeconds"
Write-Host "[->] Stop: $( $TimeLast.ToString( 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss' ))"
if ( $Line -eq $JmeterLogContent[-1] ) {
Write-Host '[cc] Copy text to the clipboard' -ForegroundColor Yellow
Set-Clipboard -Value $( $( $TimeFirst.ToString( 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss' )) + "`n" + $( $TimeLast.ToString( 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss' )))
}
Write-Host '[..] ******************************************'
$TimeLast = $null
$TimeFirst = $null
}
}

Gatling‚Äôs SBT plugin also offers four additional tasks:

Gatling/startRecorder: starts the Recorder, configured to save recorded simulations to the location specified by Gatling/scalaSource (by default, src/test/scala).
Gatling/generateReport: generates reports for a specified report folder.
Gatling/lastReport: opens by the last generated report in your web browser. A simulation name can be specified to open the last report for that simulation.
Gatling/copyConfigFiles: copies Gatling‚Äôs configuration files (gatling.conf & recorder.conf) from the bundle into your project resources if they‚Äôre missing.
Gatling/copyLogbackXml: copies Gatling‚Äôs default logback.xm
